              "    <script>\n",
              "      const buttonEl =\n",
              "        document.querySelector('#df-e289365a-22ce-4fb1-925e-fdcb733afbe8 button.colab-df-convert');\n",
              "      buttonEl.style.display =\n",
              "        google.colab.kernel.accessAllowed ? 'block' : 'none';\n",
              "\n",
              "      async function convertToInteractive(key) {\n",
              "        const element = document.querySelector('#df-e289365a-22ce-4fb1-925e-fdcb733afbe8');\n",
              "        const dataTable =\n",
              "          await google.colab.kernel.invokeFunction('convertToInteractive',\n",
              "                                                    [key], {});\n",
              "        if (!dataTable) return;\n",
              "\n",
              "        const docLinkHtml = 'Like what you see? Visit the ' +\n",
              "          '<a target=\"_blank\" href=https://colab.research.google.com/notebooks/data_table.ipynb>data table notebook</a>'\n",
              "          + ' to learn more about interactive tables.';\n",
              "        element.innerHTML = '';\n",
              "        dataTable['output_type'] = 'display_data';\n",
              "        await google.colab.output.renderOutput(dataTable, element);\n",
              "        const docLink = document.createElement('div');\n",
              "        docLink.innerHTML = docLinkHtml;\n",
              "        element.appendChild(docLink);\n",
              "      }\n",
              "    </script>\n",
              "  </div>\n",
              "\n",
              "\n",

              "        const element = document.querySelector('#df-de660e75-745b-4db8-b6ed-7bedb2cca3d3');\n",
              "        const dataTable =\n",
              "          await google.colab.kernel.invokeFunction('convertToInteractive',\n",
              "                                                    [key], {});\n",
              "        if (!dataTable) return;\n",
              "\n",
              "        const docLinkHtml = 'Like what you see? Visit the ' +\n",
              "          '<a target=\"_blank\" href=https://colab.research.google.com/notebooks/data_table.ipynb>data table notebook</a>'\n",
              "          + ' to learn more about interactive tables.';\n",
              "        element.innerHTML = '';\n",
              "        dataTable['output_type'] = 'display_data';\n",
              "        await google.colab.output.renderOutput(dataTable, element);\n",
              "        const docLink = document.createElement('div');\n",
              "        docLink.innerHTML = docLinkHtml;\n",
              "        element.appendChild(docLink);\n",
              "      }\n",
              "    </script>\n",
              "  </div>\n",
              "\n",

      "source": [
        "# Define renaming mapping for the primary columns that don't have a categorical translation replacing them directly\n",
        "colunas_para_renomear = {\n",
        "    'work_year': 'ano_trabalho',\n",
        "    'job_title': 'cargo',\n",
        "    'salary': 'salario',\n",
        "    'salary_currency': 'moeda_salario',\n",
        "    'salary_in_usd': 'salario_em_usd',\n",
        "    'employee_residence': 'residencia_empregado',\n",
        "    'company_location': 'localizacao_empresa',\n",
        "}\n",
        "\n",
        "# Apply renaming\n",
        "df = df.rename(columns=colunas_para_renomear)\n",
        "\n",
        "# Create new Portuguese categorical columns from their original English counterparts\n",
        "df[\"senioridade\"] = df[\"experience_level\"].replace({\n",
        "    'SE': 'Sênior',\n",
        "    'MI': 'Médio',\n",
        "    'EN': 'Júnior',\n",
        "    'EX': 'Executivo'\n",
        "})\n",
        "\n",
        "df['contrato'] = df['employment_type'].replace({\n",
        "    'FT': 'Tempo Integral',\n",
        "    'CT': 'Contrato',\n",
        "    'PT': 'Tempo Parcial',\n",
        "    'FL': 'Freelancer'\n",
        "})\n",
        "\n",
        "df[\"remoto\"] = df[\"remote_ratio\"].replace({\n",
        "    0: 'Presencial',\n",
        "    50: 'Híbrido',\n",
        "    100: 'Remoto'\n",
        "})\n",
        "\n",
        "df['tamanho_empresa'] = df['company_size'].replace({\n",
        "    'M': 'Médio',\n",
        "    'L': 'Grande',\n",
        "    'S': 'Pequeno'\n",
        "})\n",
        "\n",
        "\n",
        "# Columns to drop because their translated categorical versions are preferred\n",
        "colunas_para_remover = [\n",
        "    'experience_level',\n",
        "    'employment_type',\n",
        "    'remote_ratio',\n",
        "    'company_size'\n",
        "]\n",
        "\n",
        "# Drop the original English columns. Use errors='ignore' to prevent error if column already dropped/renamed\n",
        "df = df.drop(columns=[col for col in colunas_para_remover if col in df.columns], errors='ignore')\n",
        "\n",
        "# Ensure column names are unique before final selection and reordering\n",
        "df = df.loc[:,~df.columns.duplicated()]\n",
        "\n",
        "# Define the final desired order of all Portuguese columns\n",
        "colunas_finais_ordenadas = [\n",
        "    'ano_trabalho',\n",
        "    'senioridade',\n",
        "    'contrato',\n",
        "    'cargo',\n",
        "    'salario',\n",
        "    'moeda_salario',\n",
        "    'salario_em_usd',\n",
        "    'residencia_empregado',\n",
        "    'remoto',\n",
        "    'localizacao_empresa',\n",
        "    'tamanho_empresa'\n",
        "]\n",
        "\n",
        "# Reorder the DataFrame columns to match the desired final set and order\n",
        "df = df[colunas_finais_ordenadas]\n",
        "\n",
        "print(\"Colunas do DataFrame traduzidas e limpas com sucesso!\")\n",
        "print(df.columns)"
      ],

              "          '<a target=\"_blank\" href=https://colab.research.google.com/notebooks/data_table.ipynb>data table notebook</a>'\n",

              "        const docLink = document.createElement('div');\n",

              "        const dataTable =\n",

              "                                                    [key], {});\n",
              "        if (!dataTable) return;\n",
              "\n",

              "\n",
              "      async function convertToInteractive(key) {\n",
              "        const element = document.querySelector('#df-b6de3ace-e72b-4849-93b5-f0d7eaabcfea');\n",
              "        const dataTable =\n",
              "          await google.colab.kernel.invokeFunction('convertToInteractive',\n",
              "                                                    [key], {});\n",
              "        if (!dataTable) return;\n",
              "\n",
              "        const docLinkHtml = 'Like what you see? Visit the ' +\n",
              "          '<a target=\"_blank\" href=https://colab.research.google.com/notebooks/data_table.ipynb>data table notebook</a>'\n",
              "          + ' to learn more about interactive tables.';\n",
              "        element.innerHTML = '';\n",
              "        dataTable['output_type'] = 'display_data';\n",
              "        await google.colab.output.renderOutput(dataTable, element);\n",
              "        const docLink = document.createElement('div');\n",
              "        docLink.innerHTML = docLinkHtml;\n",
              "        element.appendChild(docLink);\n",
              "      }\n",
              "    </script>\n",
              "  </div>\n",
              "\n",

              "        const element = document.querySelector('#df-bf676f9d-84e3-4320-8899-17f56ab776dc');\n",
              "        const dataTable =\n",
              "          await google.colab.kernel.invokeFunction('convertToInteractive',\n",
              "                                                    [key], {});\n",
              "        if (!dataTable) return;\n",
              "\n",
              "        const docLinkHtml = 'Like what you see? Visit the ' +\n",
              "          '<a target=\"_blank\" href=https://colab.research.google.com/notebooks/data_table.ipynb>data table notebook</a>'\n",
              "          + ' to learn more about interactive tables.';\n",
              "        element.innerHTML = '';\n",
              "        dataTable['output_type'] = 'display_data';\n",
              "        await google.colab.output.renderOutput(dataTable, element);\n",
              "        const docLink = document.createElement('div');\n",
              "        docLink.innerHTML = docLinkHtml;\n",
              "        element.appendChild(docLink);\n",
              "      }\n",

      "source": [
        "import numpy as np\n",
        "\n",
        "#Criação de um dataframe de teste para usar de exemplo\n",
        "df_salarios = pd.DataFrame({\n",
        "    'nome': [\"Henrique\", \"João\", \"Maria\", \"Joaquim\", \"Val\"],\n",
        "    'salario': [4000, np.nan, 5000, np.nan, 100000]\n",
        "})\n",
        "\n",
        "#Calcula a média e substitua os nulos pela média e arredonde os valores\n",
        "df_salarios['salario_media'] = df_salarios['salario'].fillna(df_salarios['salario'].mean().round (2))\n",
        "\n",
        "'''Calcula a mediana  e substitua os nulos pela mediana\n",
        "'''\n",
        "\n",
        "df_salarios['salario_mediana'] = df_salarios['salario'].fillna(df_salarios['salario'].median())\n",
        "\n",
        "df_salarios"

              "        const element = document.querySelector('#df-7beaddfc-be6f-4a62-b570-a46d69f5608d');\n",
              "        const dataTable =\n",
              "          await google.colab.kernel.invokeFunction('convertToInteractive',\n",
              "                                                    [key], {});\n",
              "        if (!dataTable) return;\n",
              "\n",
              "        const docLinkHtml = 'Like what you see? Visit the ' +\n",
              "          '<a target=\"_blank\" href=https://colab.research.google.com/notebooks/data_table.ipynb>data table notebook</a>'\n",
              "          + ' to learn more about interactive tables.';\n",
              "        element.innerHTML = '';\n",
              "        dataTable['output_type'] = 'display_data';\n",
              "        await google.colab.output.renderOutput(dataTable, element);\n",
              "        const docLink = document.createElement('div');\n",
              "        docLink.innerHTML = docLinkHtml;\n",
              "        element.appendChild(docLink);\n",
              "      }\n",
              "    </script>\n",
              "  </div>\n",

        "# Calcular média salarial\n",
        "media_senioridade = df.groupby('senioridade')['salario_em_usd'].mean().reset_index()\n",
        "\n",
        "# Criar gráfico\n",
        "fig = px.bar(media_senioridade, x='senioridade', y='salario_em_usd',\n",
        "             title='Salário Médio por Nível de Senioridade',\n",
        "             labels={'senioridade': 'Senioridade', 'salario_em_usd': 'Salário Médio (USD)'},\n",
        "             color='senioridade')\n",
        "\n",
        "fig.update_layout(xaxis={'categoryorder': 'total descending'})\n",
        "fig.show()"

      "cell_type": "code",
      "source": [
        "import pycountry\n",
        "\n",
        "# Função para converter ISO-2 para ISO-3\n",
        "def iso2_to_iso3(code):\n",
        "    try:\n",
        "        return pycountry.countries.get(alpha_2=code).alpha_3\n",
        "    except:\n",
        "        return None\n",
        "\n",
        "# Criar nova coluna com código ISO-3\n",
        "df_limpo['residencia_iso3'] = df_limpo['residencia_empregado'].apply(iso2_to_iso3)\n",
        "\n",
        "# Calcular média salarial por país (ISO-3)\n",
        "df_ds = df_limpo[df_limpo['cargo'] == 'Data Scientist']\n",
        "media_ds_pais = df_ds.groupby('residencia_iso3')['salario_em_usd'].mean().reset_index()\n",
        "\n",
        "# Gerar o mapa\n",
        "fig = px.choropleth(media_ds_pais,\n",
        "                    locations='residencia_iso3',\n",
        "                    color='salario_em_usd',\n",
        "                    color_continuous_scale='rdylgn',\n",
        "                    title='Salário médio de Cientista de Dados por país',\n",
        "                    labels={'salario_em_usd': 'Salário médio (USD)', 'residencia_iso3': 'País'})\n",
        "\n",
        "fig.show()"
